HISTOGRAMS
==========
  Each histogram is given as 1000 pairs of values (i.e. two columns side by side).

  Possible HPD footnotes: 
       '?' HPD interval may be incorrect due to multiple peaks
       '#' HPD may not be useful - posterior density does not reach low levels near either the upper or the lower limit of the prior
